< Text>
One word describes this place-

Flavors!!

Brian prepared my family's dinner meal for us.  It was my first time there after driving by so many times for some many years from work or even from church.  I decided that I wanted to try this place out and I'm glad I did.

The short ribs were very soft and flavorful.  The vegetables were crunchy and tender but not overcooked.  I don't know how Brian did it but everything that he prepared for us and we ate was so flavorful.  All of the flavors were infused and melded together.  I also ordered the braised pork and the non spicy curry cage free chicken.  The most surprising of all was the Fiesta Combo Plate.  It reminded me of chicken sisig, a Filipino dish.  This quickly became the favorite.

I recommend to try this place out.  Their food is prepared fresh with fresh ingredients grown out front such as the herbs they used probably for making these dishes so flavorful and magical.  For sure we're coming back again in the future.</Text>

<date>1620962726466</date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
I have nothing but great things to say about my recent Taycan leasing experience with Sales Ambassador Gilbert Villagrana and Finance Ambassador Shelly Fisher III.  Both were ultra professional and helpful at every stage.  I emailed the dealership about a Taycan 4S that had just arrived, and heard back from Gilbert the same day, with a video of the car.  The next day we negotiated a very competitive lease price, and I put down a deposit to hold the car.  I then discovered I needed a bigger battery and asked Gilbert to find me a different 4S, in a hard-to-find color, with other desired options.  Diring the next two weeks he scoured all available and incoming inventory at dealerships throughout Ca and neighboring states, keeping me posted along the way.  Eventually Gilbert found just the right car coming into another dealership.

Even though Porsche Ontario needed to swap a car with a dealership hundreds of miles away to get me the one I wanted, they honored the original price we had negotiated for a car in their inventory.  The day after I signed the lease, Gilbert drove 6 hours to pick up my car at the other dealership, dropped his own car off, and then drove my car another 3 hours further to deliver it to my home.  I told him he didn't need to do that, but Gilbert wanted to configure the PCM and other systems, explain the car's features, and answer any questions I might have.  He then Ubered back to the other dealership to pick up his own car and return home.  All on a Friday!  During the next week Gilbert checked in regularly and helped answer my follow-up questions.  The Taycan is a complicated car and this proved very helpful.  How's that for going the extra mile?

Shelly was also great to deal with.  I've come to dread the usual finance department add-on pitches and hard sells.  That's not what I encountered with Shelly.  He explained the add-on packages that Porsche makes available, made straightforward recommendations about what he thought made sense for a lessee, and completely left it to me to decide with no pressure whatsoever.  Shelly also arranged for me to docu-sign all the papers and expedited completion of my lease.

I'm an attorney, I dislike surprises, and I know when someone is trying to game me. I encountered none of that.  On the contrary, I have never had a better car buying/leasing experience with any brand or dealership.   Not even close.   These gentlemen are the best, bar none.  I would do business again with either of them, and with the Porsche Ontario dealership, in a flash.

As for the Taycan 4S, it's a high spirited thing of beauty.  I  have never driven anything quite like this solid rocket. After blast off, you can just sit back and enjoy the sound system, which also delivers the best acoustic experience I've ever had.   Nice work Porsche.  Now I'm thinking 12k/year will not be enough.</Review>

< Review>
My husband is a u.s Army veteran and when we moved into our apartment a different company owned it. Regency recently purchased this property a couple months ago. First thing they did was start sending out letters about rent right away. Then followed that up with letters stating all objects had to be removed from our porches to keep the property looking nice, mind you the porch was barely big enough to hold 2 rocking chairs. Their maintenance man didn't fix anything. I had asked several times even prior to them buying the place for him to replace the window cranks and the knobs in my shower which poured a steady stream of scalding hot water.
